<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Sonate d'Involatura per Organo e Cimbalo
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Op.1
</td></tr>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>22 pieces:
<dl><dt><ul><li>Parte prima. (Organ works)
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Toccata in D&#160;minor
</dd><dd>2. Quattro versi in D&#160;minor
</dd><dd>3. Canzona in D&#160;minor
</dd><dd>4. Quattro versi in C&#160;major
</dd><dd>5. Canzona in C&#160;major
</dd><dd>6. Quattro versi in F&#160;major
</dd><dd>7. Canzona in F&#160;major
</dd><dd>8. Quattro versi in E&#160;minor
</dd><dd>9. Canzona in E&#160;minor
</dd><dd>10. Quattro versi in G&#160;minor
</dd><dd>11. Canzona in G&#160;minor
</dd><dd>12. Toccata all’Elevazione in F&#160;major
</dd><dd>13. Toccata all’post communio in F&#160;major
</dd><dd>14. Toccata all’elevazione in C&#160;major
</dd><dd>15. Toccata all’offertorio in C&#160;major
</dd><dd>16. <a href="/wiki/Pastorale_(Zipoli,_Domenico)" title="Pastorale (Zipoli, Domenico)">Pastorale in C&#160;major</a>
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Parte seconda (Harpsichord works)
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>17. <i><a href="/wiki/Keyboard_Sonata_in_B_minor,_Op.1_No.17_(Zipoli,_Domenico)" title="Keyboard Sonata in B minor, Op.1 No.17 (Zipoli, Domenico)">Keyboard Sonata in B minor</a></i>
</dd><dd>18. <i><a href="/wiki/Keyboard_Sonata_in_G_minor,_Op.1_No.18_(Zipoli,_Domenico)" title="Keyboard Sonata in G minor, Op.1 No.18 (Zipoli, Domenico)">Keyboard Sonata in G minor</a></i>
</dd><dd>19. Keyboard Sonata in C&#160;major
<dl><dd>a. Preludio; b. Allemanda; c. Sarabanda; d. Gavotta; e. Giga
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>20. Partita in C&#160;major
</dd><dd>21. Keyboard Sonata in D&#160;minor
<dl><dd>a. Preludio; b. Allemanda; c. Gavotta; d. Minuetto
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>22. <i><a href="/wiki/Partita_in_A_minor,_Op.1_No.22_(Zipoli,_Domenico)" title="Partita in A minor, Op.1 No.22 (Zipoli, Domenico)">Partita in A minor</a></i>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>His best known work but Wikipedia does not note certainly if it was first published or attached an opus number in any sense (if so, the work page name should be changed also to include the Op.1 but preferably if this can be found on a contemporary, not a modern edition.) Were these first published as a unit as early as 1716? Yes, according to L. F. Tagliavini in the preface of his 1958 edition.
</p>
